# Wave0-A File Census

Deterministic repository file census and scope classification for root + clever trees.

## Scope Rules (Precedence Order)

1. `R01`: `^clever/src/` -> `clever/src`
2. `R02`: `^clever/include/` -> `clever/include`
3. `R03`: `^clever/tests/` -> `clever/tests`
4. `R04`: `^src/` -> `src`
5. `R05`: `^include/` -> `include`
6. `R06`: `^tests/` -> `tests`
7. `R07`: docs-like path/file (`docs/`, `*.md|*.rst|*.adoc|*.txt`, or common doc basenames) -> `docs`
8. `R08`: contains path component `third_party` -> `third_party`
9. `R09`: contains path component `build` -> `build`
10. `R10`: generated markers (path component `generated`/`gen` or basename containing `generated`) -> `generated`
11. `R11`: binary extension heuristic -> `binary`
12. `R12`: metadata/config heuristic -> `metadata`
13. `R13`: fallback -> `other`

Hidden-path exclusion rule: files with any hidden path component are excluded unless doc-like (rule `R07`). `.git` is always excluded.

## Counts Per Scope

| scope | count |
|---|---:|
| `src` | 18 |
| `include` | 20 |
| `tests` | 30 |
| `docs` | 388 |
| `clever/src` | 65 |
| `clever/include` | 43 |
| `clever/tests` | 18 |
| `generated` | 0 |
| `binary` | 69 |
| `build` | 2272 |
| `metadata` | 56 |
| `third_party` | 85 |
| `other` | 8 |

Included files: 3072

Excluded files (hidden-path / .git filtering): 234
